https://maui.bluejeans.com/295235670.

MADE TO ANY MEMBER OF THE COUNCIL, STAFF OR GENERAL PUBLIC. ORAL OR WRITTEN

DELIBERATION ON EACH SECTION OF THE AGENDA. EACH TESTIFIER WILL BE ALLOWED TO SPEAK

TESTIMONY, AND NOT FOR PUBLIC COMMENTARY ON THE MEETING.\r\n\r\nIT WILL BE CONSIDERED

TO SPEAK ABOUT THE COUNCIL RULES, SO THAT COUNTY COUNCIL 23-27, AND 23-30. THE COUNTY 
COUNCIL PRIMARY DUTY IS TO PASS LAWS, LEGISLATIVE PROCESS IS OFTEN SLOW, AND THAT'S 
JUST THE WAY THAT THE FRAMERS OF THE CONSTITUTION INTENDED IT TO BE. THE FRAMERS 
BELIEVED THAT A SLOW-MOVING LEGISLATURE WOULD BE LESS ABLE TO INFRINGE ON CITIZENS' 
RIGHTS AND LIBERTIES. THE AMERICAN LEGISLATIVE PROCESS WAS DESIGNED TO BE SLOW, AND 
DIFFICULT, AND SOME MIGHT CALL IT DELIBERATIVE.\r\n\r\nTHE DESIGN WAS TO GIVE THE 
GOVERNANCE OF THE UNITED STATES OF AMERICA THE ABILITY AND PREDICTABILITY. FRAMERS 
KNEW THAT SLOW AND STEADY WAS WHAT WON THE RACE. THEY TOOK THIS IN CONTEXT OF THE  
ABUSES OF CROWN, THE BRITISH CROWN, WHICH WAS FRESH IN THE MEMORIES OF THE FRAMERS 
OF THE CONSTITUTION. SO THEY CREATED THESE CHECKS AND BALANCES, AND FURTHERMORE, 
THEY BUILT INEFFICIENCIES INTO THE LEGISLATIVE PROCESS. THE FRAMERS WERE WORRIED 
THAT THE MAJORITY OF THE GOVERNMENT TO OPPRESS THE RIGHTS OF THE MINORITY AND IN 
RESPONSE, THE FRAMERS EMPOWERED THE MAJORITY, OR RATHER MINORITY GIVEN TO DELAY 
THE LEGISLATIVE PROCESS. TO PROTECT GENERATIONS THEY ESTABLISHED AN INEFFICIENT 
SYSTEM USED BY CITIZENS ENGAGEMENT. THE PROCESS MAY BE SLOW, AND PEOPLE PROVIDE 
THE COUNTY COUNCIL WITH INPUT, THE COUNTY COUNCIL MAKES THOUGHTFUL, INFORMED AND 
DELIBERATIVE DECISIONS THAT REPRESENT AN INVESTMENT IN THE COUNTY'S FUTURE.\r\n\r\nSO 
WITH REGARDS TO 27, I JUST SUPPORT EXTENDING THE SUNSET DATE FOR THE RULES OF COUNTY 
COUNCIL, BECAUSE I THOUGHT IT WORKED QUITE WELL LAST YEAR. I WOULD LIKE TO GO ON TO 
23-30 . SO IF THE COUNCIL IS THINKING THAT ADOPTING ANY RULES, THEY SHOULD BE RULES IN 
FAVOR OF CITIZEN ENGAGEMENT, LIKE WHAT IS DONE TODAY. ALLOWING THE PUBLIC TO

MIDWIVES, TRADITIONAL MIDWIVES CPMS AND LICENSED MERCHANDISE WIVES, CPM RECEIVE 
THEIR CREDENTIALS FROM THE NORTH AMERICA REGISTRY OF MIDWIVES AND THEY CAN DO 
THAT TWO WAYS. ONE IS BY A PORTFOLIO EVALUATION PROCESS, WHERE THEY APPRENTICE WITH  
A MIDWIFE, PRECEPTOR, AND THEY SUBMIT THAT FOR ACCREDITATION THROUGH NARM AND THE 
OTHER PATHWAY IS A COLLEGE PROGRAM, AN ACCREDITED PROGRAM, AND THEN YOU SUBMIT 
THE SAME APPLICATION TO NARM AND THEY ISSUE THE SAME CPM CREDENTIAL. THOSE 
MIDWIVES CAN PRACTICE LEGALLY IN 34 STATES. IN HAWAI'I, WE GET A LICENSE ONLY THROUGH 
A CPM CREDENTIAL OBTAINED THROUGH THE PROGRAM. THAT IS THE ONLY PATHWAY.\r\n\r\nSO 
MIDWIVES MIGHT HAVE NATIONAL CREDENTIAL, BUT THEY COULD BE CRIMINALIZED UNDER THE 
LAW AND THEY COULD BE CHARGED WITH PRACTICING MIDWIFERY WITHOUT A LICENSE, EVEN

>> THANK YOU, WHEREAS, UNDER ACT 32 (2019) SECTION 457-J HAWAI'I REVISED STATUTES 
PROVIDES AN EXEMPTION THAT ALLOWS BIRTH ATTENDANTS TO ATTEND BIRTHS WITHOUT STATE  
LICENSURE, BUT THIS EXEMPTION EXPIRES JULY 1ST, 2023; AND WHEREAS, IF THE LAW EXPIRES 
TRADITIONAL AND INDIGENOUS MIDWIFERY PRACTICES WILL BE AT RISK OF CRIMINALITY OR 
WORSE, CULTURAL ERASURE; AND WHEREAS, A BIRTHING PERSON'S RIGHT TO CHOOSE WHERE TO 
GIVE BIRTH, AND WHO THEY WANT AS THEIR PREFERRED BIRTH ATTENDANT ARE INTEGRAL TO 
PROVIDING SAFETY, CARE, BODILY AUTONOMY, AND COMFORT DURING BIRTH; AND WHEREAS, 
MATERNAL MORTALITY OUTCOMES ARE DISPROPORTIONALITY HIGH AMONG BLACK, FILIPINO 
NATIVE HAWAIIAN AND PACIFIC ISLANDER BIRTHING PEOPLE; AN D WHEREAS, MIDWIFERY IS ONE 
OF THE OLDEST WOMEN'S RIGHTS HISTORY AND THE TRADITIONAL BIRTHING PRACTICES DESERVE 
PROTECTION; AND WHEREAS, AS ACT 32 (2019) NEGLECTED TO RECOGNIZE A CATEGORY OF 
CERTIFIED PROFESSIONAL MIDWIVES OR CPMS, WHO HAVE BEEN TRAINED AND CERTIFIED USING 
THE PORTFOLIO EVALUATION PROCESS THROUGH THE NATIONALLY-RECOGNIZED NORTH 
AMERICAN REGISTRY OF MIDWIVES; AND WHEREAS REQUIREMENTS FOR LICENSURE DETAILED IN 
ACT 32 (2019) ARE PROHIBITIVELY DIFFICULT FOR MANY LOCAL FAMILIES TO ACHIEVE BECAUSE 
THERE ARE CURRENTLY NO MIDWIFERY EDUCATION ACCREDITATION COUNCIL SCHOOLS IN 
HAWAI'I; AND WHEREAS, REQUIRING MIDWIFERY EDUCATION ACCREDITATION CERTIFICATION OR 
MIDWIFERY LICENSURE DISPROPORTIONATELY IMPACTS BIRTHING FAMILIES ON MOLOKA'I, ON 
LANA'I AND IN HANA, WHERE FAMILIES HAVE LIMITED ACCESS TO BIRTH FACILITIES AND HAVE 
DEPENDED ON THEIR TRADITIONAL TRAINED BIRTH ATTENDANTS FOR DECADES; AND WHEREAS, 
THE EXEMPTION ACT 32 (2019 ) FOR HEALING PRACTICES BY TRADITIONALITY HAWAIIAN HEALERS 
ENGAGED IN TRADITIONAL HEALING PRACTICES PRENATAL, MATERNAL AND CHILD-CARE 
RECOGNIZED BY COUNCIL KUPUNA CONVENED BY PAPA OLA LOKAHI IS INSUFFICIENT FOR OTHER 
CULTURES, SUCH AS NATIVE HAWAIIAN, FILIPINO, PACIFIC ISLANDER, ASIAN OR RELIGIOUS 
PRACTITIONERS OF ANY KIND; AND WHEREAS, ACT 32 (2019) SPECIFICALLY STATES, "BY THE END 
THREE-YEAR PERIOD, THE LEGISLATURE INTENDS TO ENACT STATUTES TO INCORPORATE ALL 
BIRTH PRACTITIONERS AND ALLOW THEM TO PRACTICE THAT THE FULLEST EXTENT UNDER THE 
file:///P|/OCC/LEG/Minutes/2023/230203/230203%20draft.txt[3/15/2023 9:33:10 AM]
LAW AND SENATE BILL 1047 (2023) AND HOUSE BILL 955 (2023) WOULD PERMANENTLY ALLOW 
BIRTH ATTENDANTS TO PRACTICE MIDWIFERY WITHOUT STATE LICENSURE AND FREE FROM 
CRIMINALIZATION. NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED BY THE COUNCIL OF THE COUNTY OF 
MAUI: ONE, THAT IT URGES LEGISLATURE TO ENACT A STATUTE PERMANENTLY EXEMPTING 
BIRTH ATTENDANTS FROM STATE LICENSURE REQUIREMENTS; 2, URGES LEGISLATURE TO ENACT 
STATUTE EXPANDING LICENSURE ELIGIBILITY TO INCLUDE ALL CERTIFIED PROFESSIONAL

PATHWAY; AND 3, IT AUTHORIZES AND ENCOURAGES THE COUNCIL CHAIR TO TESTIFY ON THE

BILLS WITH THE SAME PURPOSE, AND 4, THAT CERTIFIED COPIES THIS OF RESOLUTION BE

RECOGNIZE 911 EMERGENCY SERVICE DISPATCHERS ARE PART OF THE CRITICAL INFRASTRUCTURE  
OF PUBLIC SAFETY SYSTEM; AND WHEREAS, EMERGENCY SERVICES PERSONNEL PLAY A CRITICAL 
ROLE IN EMERGENCY RESPONSE AS THESE PERSONNEL ARE VERY OFTEN THE FIRST LINE OF 
COMMUNICATION FOR PERSONS NEEDING LAW ENFORCEMENT, FIRE, OR MEDICAL RESPONSE; AND  
WHEREAS, 911 EMERGENCY SERVICES DISPATCHERS ARE A LIFELINE TO LAW ENFORCEMENT, FIRE 
AND MEDICAL RESPONDERS IN THE FIELD; AND WHEREAS, 911 EMERGENCY SERVICES 
DISPATCHERS ARE RESPONSIBLE FOR AN ARRAY OF DUTIES AND SERVICES, INCLUDING 
OPERATING ADVANCED AUTOMATED TERMINALS, USING MULTIPLE LIFE-SAVING PROCEDURES 
AND TECHNOLOGIES TO OBTAIN CRITICAL INFORMATION FROM CALLERS AND ANAL YZING THE 
INFORMATION PRESENTED TO THEM AND IN SOME CASES USED SPECIALIZING MAPPING SYSTEMS 
TO SEND THE APPROPRIATE AND CLOSEST AVAILABLE UNITS AND COMMUNICATE THE BEST 
COURSE OF ACTION FOR THE CALLER TO TAKE BEFORE THE EMERGENCY UNIT ARRIVES; AND 
WHEREAS, 911 EMERGENCY SERVICES DISPATCHERS DEAL WITH IMMENSELY STRESSFUL 
SITUATIONS AS THEIR JOB RESPONSIBILITIES INCLUDE MAKING SPLIT-SECOND DECISIONS THAT 
AFFECT THE SAFETY AND WELL-BEING OF THE PUBLIC AND FIELD RESPONDERS, AND DELIVERING 
VITAL EMERGENCY PRE-ARRIVAL INSTRUCTIONS; AND WHEREAS, INFORMATION GATHERED AND 
RELAYED BY 911 EMERGENCY SERVICES DISPATCHERS CAN MEAN THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN LIFE  
AND DEATH FOR CALLERS AND FIELD RESPONDERS 911 EMERGENCY SERVICES DISPATCHERS 
PROVIDE AN INTEGRAL BASIS FOR EFFECTIVE PUBLIC SAFETY RESPONSE, AND OFTEN CAN 
PREVENT INCIDENTS FROM WORSENING BEFORE RESPONDERS ARRIVE; AND WHEREAS, ALTHOUGH  
911 EMERGENCY SERVICES DISPATCHERS ARE NOT PHYSICALLY THE SCENE OF EMERGENCIES, 
THEY OFTEN AND SUFFER FROM POST-TRAUMATIC STRESS DISORDER, AS THEIR JOB DUTIES 
INCLUDE ANSWERING MULTIPLE TRAUMATIC CALLS BONDING -- BANDING SUCCESSFUL RADIO 
INCIDENTS AND COMMUNICATING WITH PEOPLE IN STATES OF DISTRESS, FEAR, OR INJURY; AND 
WHEREAS, 911 EMERGENCY SERVICES DISPATCHERS RECEIVED SPECIALIZED TRAINING AND MUST 
WE CERTIFIED TO WORK IN 911 EMERGENCY TELECOMMUNICATIONS CENTERS; AND WHEREAS, 
STATE SENATE RESOLUTION 22-72 URGED THE COUNTIES TO RECOGNIZE 911 EMERGENCY 
SERVICES DISPATCHERS AS FIRST-RESPONDERS IN THEIR RESPECTED JURISDICTIONS; AND 
WHEREAS, THE RECOGNITION SOUGHT BY SENATE RESOLUTION 227 IS NOT WITHIN THE COUNCIL'S 
POWER TO ESTABLISH. NOW, THEREFORE, BE RESOLVED BY THE COUNCIL OF THE COUNTY OF 
MAUI: 1, THAT IT URGES THE ADMINISTRATION TO RECOGNIZE 911 EMERGENCY SERVICES 
DISPATCHERS AS FIRST-RESPONDERS IN THE COUNTY OF MAUI; AND 2, THAT CERTIFIED COPIES OF 
THIS RESOLUTION BE TRANSMITTED TO THE HONORABLE JOSH GREEN M.D., GOVERNOR , STATE OF  
HAWAI'I; THE HONORABLE RONALD KOUCHI, PRESIDENT STATE SENATE, STATE OF HAWAI'I; THE
